</span><span class="cl-8fcfcb58">sentence</span><span class="cl-8fcfcb58"> </span><span class="cl-8fcfcb58">18;sentence</span><span class="cl-8fcfcb58"> </span><span class="cl-8fcfcb58">19</span><span outcome.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fd01720"><p class="cl-8fcfd918"><span class="cl-8fcfcb44">No</span><span class="cl-8fcfcb44"> </span><span class="cl-8fcfcb44">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr class="cl-8fe276e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8fe2ba58"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">106.2</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba57"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">Turkey alone was a crisis actor, while the U.S., the USSR, and the U.K. were highly involved.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba57"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">No</span><span class="cl-8fe276e0"> </span><span class="cl-8fe276e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8fe2ba56"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">106.3</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba4c"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">BackgroundThe territories of Kars and Ardahan are located in northeast Turkey bordering Armenia.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba4c"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">No</span><span class="cl-8fe276e0"> </span><span class="cl-8fe276e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8fe2ba58"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">106.4</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba57"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">Following its defeat in the Russo/Turkish War, the Ottoman Empire transferred Kars and Ardahan to Russia in 1878.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba57"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">No</span><span class="cl-8fe276e0"> </span><span class="cl-8fe276e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8fe2ba56"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">106.5</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba4c"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">They reverted to Republican Turkey in March 1921.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba4c"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">No</span><span class="cl-8fe276e0"> </span><span class="cl-8fe276e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8fe2ba58"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">106.6</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba57"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">At the end of World War II long-standing Soviet designs on the Turkish Straits were revived when the USSR requested a revision of its 1925 alliance with Turkey -- due to changed conditions.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba57"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">No</span><span class="cl-8fe276e0"> </span><span class="cl-8fe276e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8fe2ba56"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">106.7</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba4c"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">A Soviet press campaign was launched against Turkey.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba4c"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276e0">No</span><span class="cl-8fe276e0"> </span><span class="cl-8fe276e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr Straits.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8fe2ba57"><p class="cl-8fe28342"><span class="cl-8fe276ea">Soviet</span><span class="cl-8fe276ea"> </span><span class="cl-8fe276ea">Union</span><span destroyed.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8febe1e4"><p class="cl-8febaefe"><span class="cl-8feba30a">No</span><span class="cl-8feba30a"> </span><span class="cl-8feba30a">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">The 16 November rebellion also triggered a crisis for the U.K., which perceived a threat to its influence in the Middle East.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">United</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Kingdom</span><span </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">about</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">8</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa248e"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.11</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">Britain delivered a Note to the Soviet Union on the 26th asking it to withdraw its troops from Iran by 2 March 1946.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">No</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa2490"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.12</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">A similar Note had been sent two days earlier by the U.S. setting 1 January 1946 as the date for Soviet withdrawal.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">No</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa248e"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.13</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">During the Moscow Conference of Foreign Ministers, on 19 December 1945, Foreign Secretary Bevin and Secretary of State Byrnes tried to settle the Iranian problem with Stalin.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">United</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Kingdom;United</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">States</span><span style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa2490"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.14</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">Bevin proposed that a joint commission of the Big Three be sent to Iran to investigate the Azerbaijan problem, but the proposal was rejected by the USSR.Disenchanted by the outcome of the Moscow Conference and unable to do anything within northern Iran because of Soviet interference, the Iranian government, on 19 January 1946, requested a meeting of the newly created UN Security Council, alleging that Soviet interference in Iran's internal affairs would likely cause international friction.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Soviet</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Union</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">initiated</span><span class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">The U.K.'s major response was to introduce a resolution in the Security Council on 25 January calling for bilateral negotiations between Iran and the USSR.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">United</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">United</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Nations</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span to a settlement and rejected the Council's jurisdiction in the dispute.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Soviet</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Union</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">initiated</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">reject</span><span solution.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Iran</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">initiated</span><span Moscow the deadline arrived for the evacuation of foreign troops from Iran.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">No</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa2490"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.20</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">All U.S. troops had withdrawn by 1 January 1946; and Britain had declared that its troops would be out by the stipulated date of 2 March.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">No</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa248e"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.21</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">By contrast, Radio Moscow announced on 1 March that, except for the northern provinces, Soviet forces would remain in other parts of Iran pending clarification of the situation.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">NA</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">No</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.22</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">In fact, the USSR began to pour new forces into Iran: on 4 and 5 March Soviet troops and armored columns moved outward from Tabriz in three directions -- toward the Turkish and Iraqi frontiers and toward Teheran.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa248e"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.23</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">The movement of Soviet troops in Iran, combined with an intensive Soviet diplomatic and propaganda offensive against Turkey, the main bastion against the USSR's advance into the Middle East, triggered a crisis for the United States on 4 March 1946: its global and regional influence was threatened.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">United</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">States</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">22</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa2490"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.24</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">The U.S. responded on the 7th with a decision by Byrnes to send a sharply worded protest to Moscow and to instruct the U.S. delegation to the Security Council to take a firm position on the Iranian case.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">23</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">.</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">United</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa248e"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.25</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">The Note, which was far stronger than any previous U.S. communication to the Soviet Union, was delivered in Moscow on 9 March and catalyzed a crisis for the USSR. It called on Moscow to explain Soviet troop movements and the continued presence of Soviet troops in Iran.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Soviet</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Union</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">experienced</span><span </span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">24</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa2490"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.26</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">The Soviet government, in a Tass news agency broadcast on 14 March, stated that Washington's report of troop movements was incorrect.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa248f"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e582">Soviet</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">toward</span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e"><br></span><span class="cl-8ff9e582">United</span><span class="cl-8ff9e582"> </span><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ffa248e"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">108.27</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ffa247a"><p class="cl-8ff9f144"><span class="cl-8ff9e56e">The State Department followed up its Note by declaring the same day that the U.S. would bring the dispute to the Security Council if the differences between the Soviet Union and Iran were not settled before the forthcoming Council meeting on 25 March, and if Iran itself did not raise the issue at the UN forum.</span></p></td><td 1945 when the Supreme Allied Commander for Southeast Asia announced that his troops would maintain law and order in the Netherlands East Indies until a lawful government was again functioning, and that Indonesian leader Ahmad Sukarno was to continue to direct civil administration in those areas not occupied by Allied forces.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0aa"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">experienced</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">a</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">start</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">of</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">crisis</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">about</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">speech</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">in</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">this</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">sentence</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">.</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Allies</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">initiated</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">express</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">intent</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">toward</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"><br></span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">.</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">United</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Kingdom;Allies</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">initiated</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">military</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">cooperation</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">This was regarded by the Netherlands as de facto recognition of the provisional Indonesian government and, therefore, a grave threat to its influence, long sustained by the Dutch empire.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0d2"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">experienced</span><span class="cl-9003e0aa"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">The Hague responded on 1 October with an official statement that the Netherlands would neither recognize nor negotiate with Sukarno.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0aa"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">initiated</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">109.6</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0d2"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">Indonesia's crisis was triggered on 2 October by the arrival of a Dutch administrator and the landing of additional Dutch forces, interpreted by the Indonesians as a Dutch effort to restore colonial rule.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0d2"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">109.7</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0aa"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">Severe fighting ensued between nationalist and Dutch and British forces.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0aa"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Indonesia</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">initiated</span><span style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9003e0d3"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">109.8</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0d2"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">On 13 October 1945 Indonesia responded with a declaration of war against the Netherlands and the prohibition of the sale of food to the enemy.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0d2"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Indonesia</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">initiated</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span dispute.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0d2"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">United</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Kingdom</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">With Kerr present, mediation began on 10 February 1946 between Indonesian Prime Minister Sjahrir and Dr. Van Mook of the Netherlands.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0aa"><p differences between the sides.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0d2"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">No</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">United</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Kingdom</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span until March of 1947.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0aa"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">United</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span establishment of a Truce Supervisory Committee composed of Dutch, British, and Indonesian representatives, and the creation of the United States of Indonesia linked to the Netherlands.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0d2"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Indonesia</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8"> </span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">experienced</span><span </span><span class="cl-9003a9dc">17</span><span class="cl-9003a9c8">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9003e0c8"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">109.19</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0aa"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9c8">The UN Security Council was involved because of a joint USSR-Ukrainian complaint on the issue of Dutch military intervention.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9003e0aa"><p class="cl-9003b544"><span class="cl-9003a9dc">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9003a9dc"> </span><span
